Harry Potter, Sawyer argues, neither faces a "moral struggle" nor undergoes any ethical growth, and is thus "no guide in circumstances in which right and wrong are anything less than black and white". HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-117" [117] In contrast Emily Griesinger described Harry's first passage through to HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Platform_9%C2%BE" \o "Platform 9¾" Platform 9¾ as an application of faith and hope, and his encounter with the Sorting Hat as the first of many in which Harry is shaped by the choices he makes. She also noted the "deeper magic" by which the self-sacrifice of Harry's mother protects the boy throughout the series, and which the power-hungry  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Voldemort" \o "Voldemort" Voldemort fails to understand. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-118" [118]In an 8 November 2002  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slate_(magazine)" \o "Slate (magazine)" Slate article, Chris Suellentrop likened Potter to a "trust-fund kid whose success at school is largely attributable to the gifts his friends and relatives lavish upon him". Noting that in Rowling's fiction, magical ability potential is "something you are born to, not something you can achieve", Suellentrop wrote that Dumbledore's maxim that "It is our choices that show what we truly are, far more than our abilities" is hypocritical, as "the school that Dumbledore runs values native gifts above all else". HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-119" [119] In a 12 August 2007 New York Times review of Deathly Hallows, however,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Hitchens" \o "Christopher Hitchens" Christopher Hitchens praised Rowling for "unmooring" her "English school story" from literary precedents "bound up with dreams of wealth and class and snobbery", arguing that she had instead created "a world of youthful democracy and diversity". HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-120" [120]ControversiesMain articles:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Legal_disputes_over_the_Harry_Potter_series" \o "Legal disputes over the Harry Potter series" Legal disputes over the Harry Potter series,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Religious_debates_over_the_Harry_Potter_series" \o "Religious debates over the Harry Potter series" Religious debates over the Harry Potter series,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Politics_of_Harry_Potter" \o "Politics of Harry Potter" Politics of Harry Potter, and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tanya_Grotter" \o "Tanya Grotter" Tanya GrotterThe books have been the subject of a number of  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lawsuit" \o "Lawsuit" legal proceedings, stemming either from claims by American Christian groups that the magic in the books promotes  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wicca" \o "Wicca" Wicca and witchcraft among children, or from various conflicts over copyright and trademark infringements. The popularity and high  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Market_value" \o "Market value" market value of the series has led Rowling, her publishers, and film distributor  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warner_Bros." \o "Warner Bros." Warner Bros. to take legal measures to protect their copyright, which have included banning the sale of Harry Potter imitations, targeting the owners of websites over the "Harry Potter"  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain_name" \o "Domain name" domain name, and suing author  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nancy_Stouffer" \o "Nancy Stouffer" Nancy Stouffer to counter her accusations that Rowling had plagiarised her work. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-121" [121] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-122" [122] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-123" [123] Various religious conservatives have claimed that the books promote witchcraft and religions such as  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wicca" \o "Wicca" Wicca and are therefore unsuitable for children, HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-124" [124] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-125" [125] while a number of critics have criticised the books for promoting various political agendas. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-126" [126] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-127" [127]The books also aroused controversies in the literary and publishing worlds. In 1997 to 1998,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" \o "Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone" Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone won almost all the UK awards judged by children, but none of the children's book awards judged by adults, HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-Eccleshare2002GuidePublishing-128" [128] and Sandra Beckett suggested the reason was  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Intellectual_snobbery" \o "Intellectual snobbery" intellectual snobbery towards books that were popular among children. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-Beckett2008Crossover-129" [129] In 1999, the winner of the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Whitbread_Book_Award" \o "Whitbread Book Award" Whitbread Book of the Year Award children's division was entered for the first time on the shortlist for the main award, and one judge threatened to resign if  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" \o "Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban" Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban was declared the overall winner; it finished second, very close behind the winner of the poetry prize, HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seamus_Heaney" \o "Seamus Heaney" Seamus Heaney's translation of the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Saxon" \o "Anglo-Saxon" Anglo-Saxon  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Epic_poetry" \o "Epic poetry" epic  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beowulf" \o "Beowulf" Beowulf. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-Beckett2008Crossover-129" [129]In 2000, shortly before the publication of  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" \o "Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire" Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire, the previous three Harry Potter books topped the New York Times fiction best-seller list and a third of the entries were children's books. The newspaper created a new children's section covering children's books, including both fiction and non-fiction, and initially counting only hardback sales. The move was supported by publishers and booksellers. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-NYT_2000.2F06.2F24-83" [83] In 2004, The New York Times further split the children's list, which was still dominated by Harry Potterbooks into sections for series and individual books, and removed the Harry Potter books from the section for individual books. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-130" [130] The split in 2000 attracted condemnation, praise and some comments that presented both benefits and disadvantages of the move. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-131" [131] Time suggested that, on the same principle, Billboard should have created a separate " HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mop-top" \o "Mop-top" mop-tops" list in 1964 when the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beatles" \o "Beatles" Beatles held the top five places in its list, and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nielsen_Media_Research" \o "Nielsen Media Research" Nielsen should have created a separate game-show list when  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Who_Wants_to_Be_a_Millionaire%3F" \o "Who Wants to Be a Millionaire?" Who Wants to Be a Millionaire? dominated the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nielsen_ratings" \o "Nielsen ratings" ratings. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-132" [132]AdaptationsFilmsMain article:  sold the film rights of the first four Harry Potter books to  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warner_Bros." \o "Warner Bros." Warner Bros. for a reported £1 million ($1,982,900). HYPERLINK Terry Gilliam,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Demme" \o "Jonathan Demme" Jonathan Demme, and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alan_Parker" \o "Alan Parker" Alan HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" \o "Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (film)" Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (titled Home Alone and HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mrs._Doubtfire" \o "Mrs. Doubtfire" Mrs. Doubtfire and proven experience with directing children as influences for their decision. Filming was completed in summer 2002, with the film being released on 15 November 2002. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-139" [139]  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daniel_Radcliffe" \o "Daniel Radcliffe" Daniel Radcliffe portrayed  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_(character)" \o "Harry Potter (character)" Harry Potter, doing so for all succeeding films in the franchise.Columbus declined to direct  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" \o "Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)" Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban, only acting as producer. Mexican director  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfonso_Cuar%C3%B3n" \o "Alfonso Cuarón" Alfonso Cuarón took over the job, and after shooting in 2003, the film was released on 4 June 2004. Due to the fourth film beginning its production before the third's release,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mike_Newell_(director)" \o "Mike Newell (director)" Mike Newell was chosen as the director for  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" \o "Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)" Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire, released on 18 November 2005. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-140" [140] Newell became the first British director of the series, with television director  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Yates" \o "David Yates" David Yates following suit after he was chosen to helm HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" \o "Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)" Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix. Production began in January 2006 and the film was released the following year in July 2007. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-141" [141] After executives were "really delighted" with his work on the film, Yates was selected to direct  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" \o "Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)" Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince, which was released on 15 July 2009. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-142" [142] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-yates-director-scifi-143" [143] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-date_change-144" [144] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-release-date-hbp-film-145" [145] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank_2.jpg"  INCLUDEPICTURE "http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank_2.jpg/170px-Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank_2.jpg" \* MERGEFORMATINET  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank_2.jpg" \o "Enlarge"  INCLUDEPICTURE "http://bits.wikimedia.org/static-1.24wmf1/skins/common/images/magnify-clip.png" \* MERGEFORMATINET Gringotts Wizarding Bank as seen in the film series.In March 2008, Warner Bros. Deathly Hallows, would be released in two cinematic parts:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows_%E2%80%93_Part_1" \o "Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 1" Part 1 on 19 November 2010 and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows_%E2%80%93_Part_2" \o "Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 2" Part 2 on in February 2009, with the final day of principal photography taking place on 12 June 2010. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-146" [146] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-147" [147]Rowling had creative control on the film series, observing the filmmaking process of Philosopher's Stone and serving as producer on the two-partDeathly Hallows, alongside  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Heyman" \o "David Heyman" David Heyman and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Barron_(film_producer)" \o "David Barron (film producer)" David Barron. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-148" [148] The Harry Potter films have been top-rank box office hits, with all eight releases on the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_highest-grossing_films" \o "List of highest-grossing films" list of highest-grossing films worldwide. Philosopher's Stone was the highest-grossing Harry Potter film up until the release of the final instalment of the series, Deathly Hallows, while Prisoner of Azkaban grossed the least. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-149" [149] As well as being a financial success, the film series has also been a  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Critical_response_to_the_Harry_Potter_films&action=edit&redlink=1" \o "Critical response to the Harry Potter films (page does not exist)" success among film critics. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-150" [150] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-151" [151]Opinions of the films are generally divided among fans, with one group preferring the more faithful approach of the first two films, and another group preferring the more stylised character-driven approach of the later films. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-152" [152] Rowling has been constantly supportive of all the films and evaluated Deathly Hallows as her "favourite one" in the series. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-jk-on-ps-film-153" [153] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-jk-on-poa-film-154" [154] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-jk-on-gof-film-155" [155] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-156" [156] She wrote on her website of the changes in the book-to-film transition, "It is simply impossible to incorporate every one of my storylines into a film that has to be kept under four hours long. Obviously films have restrictions novels do not have, constraints of time and budget; I can create dazzling effects relying on nothing but the interaction of my own and my readers' imaginations". HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-157" [157]At the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/64th_British_Academy_Film_Awards" \o "64th British Academy Film Awards" 64th British Academy Film Awards in February 2011, Rowling was joined by producers David Heyman and David Barron along with directors David Yates, Alfonso Cuarón and Mike Newell in collecting the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/64th_British_Academy_Film_Awards" \l "Michael_Balcon_Award_for_Outstanding_British_Contribution_to_Cinema" \o "64th British Academy Film Awards" Michael Balcon Award for Outstanding British Contribution to Cinema on behalf of all the films in the series. Actors  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rupert_Grint" \o "Rupert Grint" Rupert Grint and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emma_Watson" \o "Emma Watson" Emma Watson, who play main characters  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ron_Weasley" \o "Ron Weasley" Ron Weasley and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hermione_Granger" \o "Hermione Granger" Hermione Granger, were also in attendance. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-158" [158] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-159" [159]GamesThere are eleven Harry Potter video games, eight of which correspond with the films and books, and three other spin-offs. The film/book based games are produced by  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Electronic_Arts" \o "Electronic Arts" Electronic Arts, as was  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Quidditch_World_Cup" \o "Harry Potter: Quidditch World Cup" Harry Potter: Quidditch World Cup, with the game version of the first entry in the series,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (video game)" Philosopher's Stone, being released in November 2001. The video games are released to coincide with the films, containing scenery and details from the films as well as the tone and spirit of the books. Objectives usually occur in and around  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hogwarts" \o "Hogwarts" Hogwarts, along with various other magical areas. The story and design of the games follows the selected film's characterisation and plot; EA worked closely with Warner Brothers to include scenes from the films. The last game in the series, Deathly Hallows, was split with  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows_-_Part_1_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows - Part 1 (video game)" Part 1 released in November 2010 and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows_-_Part_2_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows - Part 2 (video game)" Part 2 debuting on consoles in July 2011. The two-part game forms the first entry to convey an intense theme of action and violence, with the gameplay revolving around a third-person shooter style format. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-160" [160] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-161" [161] The other spin-offs games,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1%E2%80%934" \o "LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1–4" LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1–4 and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lego_Harry_Potter:_Years_5%E2%80%937" \o "Lego Harry Potter: Years 5–7" LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5–7 are developed by  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Traveller%27s_Tales" \o "Traveller's Tales" Traveller's Tales and published by  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warner_Bros._Interactive_Entertainment" \o "Warner Bros. Interactive Entertainment" Warner Bros. Interactive Entertainment. A number of other non-interactive media games have been released; board games such as  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cluedo" \o "Cluedo" Cluedo Harry Potter Edition,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scene_It%3F" \o "Scene It?" Scene It? Harry Potter and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lego_Harry_Potter" \o "Lego Harry Potter" Lego Harry Potter models, which are influenced by the themes of both the novels and films.2001:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (video game)" Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone2002:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (video game)" Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets2004:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (video game)" Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban2005:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (video game)" Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire2007:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (video game)" Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix2009:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (video game)" Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince2010:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows_%E2%80%93_Part_1_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 1 (video game)" Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 12011:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows_%E2%80%93_Part_2_(video_game)" \o "Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 2 (video game)" Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows – Part 2AudiobooksAll seven Harry Potter books have been released in unabridged audiobook versions, with  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Fry" \o "Stephen Fry" Stephen Fry reading for listeners in the UK, and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jim_Dale" \o "Jim Dale" Jim Dale voicing the series for the American editions. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-162" [162] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-163" [163]Stage productionOn 20 December 2013 J. K. Rowling announced that she was working on a Harry Potter–based play for which she would be one of the producers. In her statement, the author said that the play will "explore the previously untold story of Harry's early years as an orphan and outcast". British theatre producers  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sonia_Friedman" \o "Sonia Friedman" Sonia Friedman and  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colin_Callender" \o "Colin Callender" Colin Callender will be the co-producers. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-164" [164] HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-165" [165]AttractionsUnited StatesMain article:  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Wizarding_World_of_Harry_Potter_(Islands_of_Adventure)" \o "The Wizarding World of Harry Potter (Islands of Adventure)" The Wizarding World of Harry Potter (Islands of Adventure) HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Wizarding_World_of_Harry_Potter_Castle.jpg"  INCLUDEPICTURE "http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Wizarding_World_of_Harry_Potter_Castle.jpg/220px-Wizarding_World_of_Harry_Potter_Castle.jpg" \* MERGEFORMATINET  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Wizarding_World_of_Harry_Potter_Castle.jpg" \o "Enlarge"  INCLUDEPICTURE "http://bits.wikimedia.org/static-1.24wmf1/skins/common/images/magnify-clip.png" \* MERGEFORMATINET Hogwarts Castle as depicted in the Wizarding World of Harry Potter located in Universal Orlando Resort's Island of Adventure.After the success of the films and books, Universal and Warner Brothers announced they would create "The Wizarding World of Harry Potter," a new Harry Potter-themed expansion to the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Islands_of_Adventure" \o "Islands of Adventure" Islands of Adventure theme park at  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Universal_Orlando_Resort" \o "Universal Orlando Resort" Universal Orlando Resort in Florida. The new land, promoted as the seventh themed "island" of the park, was built from land reserved for expansion outside of the park's original border, as well as from much of the existing "island,"  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mythos_(restaurant)" \o "Mythos (restaurant)" The Lost Continent. A soft opening was held at the end of March 2010, with the land opening on 16 June 2010 for reserved guests. The land officially opened to the public on 18 June 2010. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-166" [166]Guests enter the land through a recreation of the Hogsmeade station, HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-167" [167] leading into the village of  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hogsmeade" \o "Hogsmeade" Hogsmeade, with a  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forced_perspective" \o "Forced perspective" forced-perspectiveHogwarts castle at the very end of the street. The castle contains the expansion's centrepiece attraction, Harry Potter & the Forbidden Journey, a  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/KUKA" \o "KUKA" KUKA arm attraction which takes passengers through many realistic scenes influenced by the movies and books, including soaring over Hogwarts, getting involved in a Quidditch match, and having close encounters with dragons, dementors, and the Whomping Willow. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-168" [168] Other attractions include a twin high-speed rollercoaster named the  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dragon_Challenge" \o "Dragon Challenge" Dragon Challenge, a renovation of the previously existing rollercoaster,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dueling_Dragons" \o "Dueling Dragons" Dueling Dragons, and a family roller coaster called  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Flight_of_the_Hippogriff" \o "Flight of the Hippogriff" Flight of the Hippogriff, a renovation of the previously existing ride,  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Flight_of_the_Hippogriff" \l "Flying_Unicorn_era" \o "Flight of the Hippogriff" Flying Unicorn. In addition to the three rides are several themed shops and restaurants, heavily inspired by their appearances in the books and films: Honeydukes sells sweets, such as chocolate frogs and Bertie Bott's Every-Flavour Beans, Ollivander's offers personalised magic wands, Zonko's Joke Shop sells various items including Sneakoscopes, and the Three Broomsticks serves food and drink, most notably Butterbeer and pumpkin juice.Developed at a cost of $265 million, the new land "has seen capacity crowds [and] waits of up to two hours just to enter the ... merchandise shop." Islands of Adventure saw a massive increase in attendance following the expansion, seeing gains of as much as 36%, HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-169" [169] a period during which attendance to competitor resort  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walt_Disney_World" \o "Walt Disney World" Walt Disney World dropped slightly. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-170" [170] Disney had itself entered negotiations for a Harry Potter-themed expansion, but ultimately turned down the opportunity. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-171" [171]United KingdomIn March 2011, Warner Bros. announced plans to build a tourist attraction in the United Kingdom to showcase the Harry Potter film series. Warner Bros. Studio Tour London is a behind-the-scenes walking tour featuring authentic sets, costumes and props from the film series. The attraction is located at  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warner_Bros._Studios,_Leavesden" \o "Warner Bros. Studios, Leavesden" Warner Bros. Studios, Leavesden, where all eight of the Harry Potter films were made. Warner Bros. constructed two new sound stages to house and showcase the famous sets from each of the British-made productions, following a £100 million investment. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-172" [172] It opened to the public in March 2012. HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_note-173" [173]See also INCLUDEPICTURE "http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Office-book.svg/30px-Office-book.svg.png" \* MERGEFORMATINET  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book:Harry_Potter" \o "Book:Harry Potter" Book: Harry Potter HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mary_GrandPr%C3%A9" \o "Mary GrandPré" Mary GrandPré HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Tom_Sawyer_1876_frontispiece.jpg"  INCLUDEPICTURE "http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Tom_Sawyer_1876_frontispiece.jpg/15px-Tom_Sawyer_1876_frontispiece.jpg" \* MERGEFORMATINET  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portal:Children%27s_literature" \o "Portal:Children's literature" Children's literature portal  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:HP_-_Harry_Potter_wordmark.svg"  INCLUDEPICTURE "http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/HP_-_Harry_Potter_wordmark.svg/19px-HP_-_Harry_Potter_wordmark.svg.png" \* MERGEFORMATINET  HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portal:Harry_Potter" \o "Portal:Harry Potter" Harry Potter portalReferences HYPERLINK "http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter" \l "cite_ref-1" Jump up^ PETER SVENSSON 27 March 2012 (27 March 2012).  HYPERLINK "http://news.yahoo.com/harry-potter-breaks-e-book-lockdown-205343680.html" "Harry Potter breaks e-book lockdown - Yahoo!
